# Activity Log

## 2026-02-06
- Verified project path: `/mnt/Data/PopOS/Data_Ana/Wu/clawdPorjects/HADDOCK_test`.
- Inputs present: `data/receptor.pdb`, `data/ligand.pdb`, `restraints/air_all.tbl`.
- Added chain-merge helper: `scripts/merge_chains.py`.
- Added splitter/prep helper: `scripts/prepare_from_complex.py` (finds receptor chains from `pdbAG/<name>.pdb` after stripping `refold_` prefix/`_Epi` suffix; splits complex, then merges chains into single-chain receptor/ligand).
- Added batch pipeline: `scripts/run_pipeline.py` (per-complex split/merge, intra-lig lock, interface AIRs, per-config generation, per-base logs under docs/pipeline_logs/, auto-run haddock3, archive artifacts, clean intermediates).
- Generated merged single-chain inputs: `data/receptor_single.pdb` (A, renumbered) and `data/ligand_single.pdb` (X, H+L merged, renumbered).
- Config defaults updated: ncores=20, sampling=20 for rigidbody; intermediates cleaned from data/ after run; artifacts archived under results/run_<base>/.
- Added intra-ligand lock restraints: `restraints/intra_lig_lock.tbl` (12 closest CA–CA contacts across original H/L interface) to keep heavy/light orientation fixed.
- Regenerated AIRs for merged ligand chain X: `restraints/air_all.tbl` now links receptor hotspots (B-factor > -20) to ligand interface residues (X32, X33, X101, X102) from the starting complex.
- Updated run config `docs/haddock3_config_region.cfg`:
  - molecules = receptor_single.pdb, ligand_single.pdb
  - ncores = 1, sampling = 2 (minimal test)
  - ambig_fname = restraints/air_all.tbl (A ↔ X interface)
  - unambig_fname = restraints/intra_lig_lock.tbl for rigidbody/flexref/emref
  - mol_fix_origin_1/2 = false
- Note: venv at `.venv` with `pip install -e /home/yiran/BioTools/haddock3`.
- Runs still killed at flexref (signal 9) even with low sampling; merged ligand plus intra-lig lock prepared to minimize internal drift.
